\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00003}00003 \textcolor{comment}{// This library helps render large-\/scale "{}voxel"{} worlds for games,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00004}00004 \textcolor{comment}{// in this case, one with blocks that can have textures and that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00005}00005 \textcolor{comment}{// can also be a few shapes other than cubes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00006}00006 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00007}00007 \textcolor{comment}{//    Video introduction:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00008}00008 \textcolor{comment}{//       http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2vnTtiLrV1w}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00009}00009 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00010}00010 \textcolor{comment}{//    Minecraft-\/viewer sample app (not very simple though):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00011}00011 \textcolor{comment}{//       http://github.com/nothings/stb/tree/master/tests/caveview}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00012}00012 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00013}00013 \textcolor{comment}{// It works by creating triangle meshes. The library includes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00014}00014 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00015}00015 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ converter from dense 3D arrays of block info to vertex mesh}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00016}00016 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ vertex \& fragment shaders for the vertex mesh}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00017}00017 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ assistance in setting up shader state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00018}00018 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00019}00019 \textcolor{comment}{// For portability, none of the library code actually accesses}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00020}00020 \textcolor{comment}{// the 3D graphics API. (At the moment, it's not actually portable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00021}00021 \textcolor{comment}{// since the shaders are GLSL only, but patches are welcome.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00022}00022 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00023}00023 \textcolor{comment}{// You have to do all the caching and tracking of vertex buffers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00024}00024 \textcolor{comment}{// yourself. However, you could also try making a game with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00025}00025 \textcolor{comment}{// a small enough world that it's fully loaded rather than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00026}00026 \textcolor{comment}{// streaming. Currently the preferred vertex format is 20 bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00027}00027 \textcolor{comment}{// per quad. There are designs to allow much more compact formats}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00028}00028 \textcolor{comment}{// with a slight reduction in shader features, but no roadmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00029}00029 \textcolor{comment}{// for actually implementing them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00030}00030 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00031}00031 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00032}00032 \textcolor{comment}{// USAGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00033}00033 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00034}00034 \textcolor{comment}{//   \#define the symbol STB\_VOXEL\_RENDER\_IMPLEMENTATION in *one*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00035}00035 \textcolor{comment}{//   C/C++ file before the \#include of this file; the implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00036}00036 \textcolor{comment}{//   will be generated in that file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00037}00037 \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00039}00039 \textcolor{comment}{//   implementation will be private to that file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00040}00040 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00041}00041 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00042}00042 \textcolor{comment}{// FEATURES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00043}00043 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00044}00044 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ you can choose textured blocks with the features below,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00045}00045 \textcolor{comment}{//     or colored voxels with 2\string^24 colors and no textures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00046}00046 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00047}00047 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ voxels are mostly just cubes, but there's support for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00048}00048 \textcolor{comment}{//     half-\/height cubes and diagonal slopes, half-\/height}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00049}00049 \textcolor{comment}{//     diagonals, and even odder shapes especially for doing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00050}00050 \textcolor{comment}{//     more-\/continuous "{}ground"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00051}00051 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00052}00052 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ texture coordinates are projections along one of the major}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00053}00053 \textcolor{comment}{//     axes, with the per-\/texture scaling.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00054}00054 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00055}00055 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ a number of aspects of the shader and the vertex format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00056}00056 \textcolor{comment}{//     are configurable; the library generally takes care of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00057}00057 \textcolor{comment}{//     coordinating the vertex format with the mesh for you.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00058}00058 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00059}00059 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00060}00060 \textcolor{comment}{// FEATURES (SHADER PERSPECTIVE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00061}00061 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00062}00062 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ vertices aligned on integer lattice, z on multiples of 0.5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00063}00063 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ per-\/vertex "{}lighting"{} or "{}ambient occlusion"{} value (6 bits)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00064}00064 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ per-\/vertex texture crossfade (3 bits)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00065}00065 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00066}00066 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ per-\/face texture \#1 id (8-\/bit index into array texture)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00067}00067 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ per-\/face texture \#2 id (8-\/bit index into second array texture)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00068}00068 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ per-\/face color (6-\/bit palette index, 2 bits of per-\/texture boolean enable)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00069}00069 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ per-\/face 5-\/bit normal for lighting calculations \& texture coord computation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00070}00070 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ per-\/face 2-\/bit texture matrix rotation to rotate faces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00071}00071 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00072}00072 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ indexed-\/by-\/texture-\/id scale factor (separate for texture \#1 and texture \#2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00073}00073 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ indexed-\/by-\/texture-\/\#2-\/id blend mode (alpha composite or modulate/multiply);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00074}00074 \textcolor{comment}{//     the first is good for decals, the second for detail textures, "{}light maps"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00075}00075 \textcolor{comment}{//     etc; both modes are controlled by texture \#2's alpha, scaled by the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00076}00076 \textcolor{comment}{//     per-\/vertex texture crossfade and the per-\/face color (if enabled on texture \#2);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{//     modulate/multiply multiplies by an extra factor of 2.0 so that if you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{//     make detail maps whose average brightness is 0.5 everything works nicely.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00080}00080 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ ambient lighting: half-\/lambert directional plus constant, all scaled by vertex ao}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00081}00081 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ face can be fullbright (emissive), controlled by per-\/face color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00082}00082 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ installable lighting, with default single-\/point-\/light}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ installable fog, with default hacked smoothstep}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00084}00084 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{//  Note that all the variations of lighting selection and texture}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{//  blending are run-\/time conditions in the shader, so they can be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00087}00087 \textcolor{comment}{//  intermixed in a single mesh.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{// INTEGRATION ARC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00091}00091 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{//   The way to get this library to work from scratch is to do the following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00094}00094 \textcolor{comment}{//      Step 1. define STBVOX\_CONFIG\_MODE to 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{//        This mode uses only vertex attributes and uniforms, and is easiest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{//        to get working. It requires 32 bytes per quad and limits the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{//        size of some tables to avoid hitting uniform limits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{//      Step 2. define STBVOX\_CONFIG\_MODE to 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{//        This requires using a texture buffer to store the quad data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{//        reducing the size to 20 bytes per quad.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{//      Step 3: define STBVOX\_CONFIG\_PREFER\_TEXBUFFER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{//        This causes some uniforms to be stored as texture buffers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{//        instead. This increases the size of some of those tables,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{//        and avoids a potential slow path (gathering non-\/uniform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{//        data from uniforms) on some hardware.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{//   In the future I might add additional modes that have significantly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{//   smaller meshes but reduce features, down as small as 6 bytes per quad.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{//   See elsewhere in this file for a table of candidate modes. Switching}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{//   to a mode will require changing some of your mesh creation code, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{//   everything else should be seamless. (And I'd like to change the API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{//   so that mesh creation is data-\/driven the way the uniforms are, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{//   then you wouldn't even have to change anything but the mode number.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{// IMPROVEMENTS FOR SHIP-\/WORTHY PROGRAMS USING THIS LIBRARY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{//   I currently tolerate a certain level of "{}bugginess"{} in this library.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{//   I'm referring to things which look a little wrong (as long as they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{//   don't cause holes or cracks in the output meshes), or things which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{//   do not produce as optimal a mesh as possible. Notable examples:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/  incorrect lighting on slopes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/  inefficient meshes for vheight blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{//   I am willing to do the work to improve these things if someone is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{//   going to ship a substantial program that would be improved by them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{//   (It need not be commercial, nor need it be a game.) I just didn't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{//   want to do the work up front if it might never be leveraged. So just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{//   submit a bug report as usual (github is preferred), but add a note}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{//   that this is for a thing that is really going to ship. (That means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{//   you need to be far enough into the project that it's clear you're}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{//   committed to it; not during early exploratory development.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00142}00142 \textcolor{comment}{// VOXEL MESH API}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{//   Context}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00145}00145 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{//     To understand the API, make sure you first understand the feature set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{//     listed above.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00148}00148 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00149}00149 \textcolor{comment}{//     Because the vertices are compact, they have very limited spatial}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00150}00150 \textcolor{comment}{//     precision. Thus a single mesh can only contain the data for a limited}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00151}00151 \textcolor{comment}{//     area. To make very large voxel maps, you'll need to build multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00152}00152 \textcolor{comment}{//     vertex buffers. (But you want this anyway for frustum culling.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00153}00153 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{//     Each generated mesh has three components:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00155}00155 \textcolor{comment}{//             -\/ vertex data (vertex buffer)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{//             -\/ face data (optional, stored in texture buffer)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{//             -\/ mesh transform (uniforms)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{//     Once you've generated the mesh with this library, it's up to you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{//     to upload it to the GPU, to keep track of the state, and to render}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{//     it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00162}00162 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00163}00163 \textcolor{comment}{//   Concept}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00164}00164 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00165}00165 \textcolor{comment}{//     The basic design is that you pass in one or more 3D arrays; each array}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00166}00166 \textcolor{comment}{//     is (typically) one-\/byte-\/per-\/voxel and contains information about one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00167}00167 \textcolor{comment}{//     or more properties of some particular voxel property.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00169}00169 \textcolor{comment}{//     Because there is so much per-\/vertex and per-\/face data possible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00170}00170 \textcolor{comment}{//     in the output, and each voxel can have 6 faces and 8 vertices, it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00171}00171 \textcolor{comment}{//     would require an very large data structure to describe all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00172}00172 \textcolor{comment}{//     of the possibilities, and this would cause the mesh-\/creation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00173}00173 \textcolor{comment}{//     process to be slow. Instead, the API provides multiple ways}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00174}00174 \textcolor{comment}{//     to express each property, some more compact, others less so;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00175}00175 \textcolor{comment}{//     each such way has some limitations on what it can express.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00176}00176 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00177}00177 \textcolor{comment}{//     Note that there are so many paths and combinations, not all of them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00178}00178 \textcolor{comment}{//     have been tested. Just report bugs and I'll fix 'em.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00179}00179 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00180}00180 \textcolor{comment}{//   Details}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00181}00181 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00182}00182 \textcolor{comment}{//     See the API documentation in the header-\/file section.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00264}00264 \textcolor{comment}{//  \#define STBVOX\_CONFIG\_PRECISION\_Z  <integer>   // OPTIONAL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00265}00265 \textcolor{comment}{//     Defines the number of bits of fractional position for Z.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00266}00266 \textcolor{comment}{//     Only 0 or 1 are valid. 1 is the default. If 0, then a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00267}00267 \textcolor{comment}{//     single mesh has twice the legal Z range; e.g. in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00268}00268 \textcolor{comment}{//     modes 0,1,20,21, Z in the mesh can extend to 511 instead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00269}00269 \textcolor{comment}{//     of 255. However, half-\/height blocks cannot be used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00270}00270 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00271}00271 \textcolor{comment}{// All of the following are just \#ifdef tested so need no values, and are optional.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00281}00281 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00282}00282 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_PREFER\_TEXBUFFER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00283}00283 \textcolor{comment}{//        Stores many of the uniform arrays in texture buffers instead,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00284}00284 \textcolor{comment}{//        so they can be larger and may be more efficient on some hardware.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00285}00285 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00286}00286 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_LIGHTING\_SIMPLE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00287}00287 \textcolor{comment}{//        Creates a simple lighting engine with a single point light source}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00288}00288 \textcolor{comment}{//        in addition to the default half-\/lambert ambient light.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00289}00289 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00290}00290 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_LIGHTING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00291}00291 \textcolor{comment}{//        Declares a lighting function hook; you must append a lighting function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00292}00292 \textcolor{comment}{//        to the shader before compiling it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00293}00293 \textcolor{comment}{//            vec3 compute\_lighting(vec3 pos, vec3 norm, vec3 albedo, vec3 ambient);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00294}00294 \textcolor{comment}{//        'ambient' is the half-\/lambert ambient light with vertex ambient-\/occlusion applied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00295}00295 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00296}00296 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_FOG\_SMOOTHSTEP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00297}00297 \textcolor{comment}{//        Defines a simple unrealistic fog system designed to maximize}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00298}00298 \textcolor{comment}{//        unobscured view distance while not looking too weird when things}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00299}00299 \textcolor{comment}{//        emerge from the fog. Configured using an extra array element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00300}00300 \textcolor{comment}{//        in the STBVOX\_UNIFORM\_ambient uniform.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00301}00301 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00302}00302 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_FOG}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00303}00303 \textcolor{comment}{//        Defines a fog function hook; you must append a fog function to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00304}00304 \textcolor{comment}{//        the shader before compiling it:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00305}00305 \textcolor{comment}{//            vec3 compute\_fog(vec3 color, vec3 relative\_pos, float fragment\_alpha);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00306}00306 \textcolor{comment}{//        "{}color"{} is the incoming pre-\/fogged color, fragment\_alpha is the alpha value,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00307}00307 \textcolor{comment}{//        and relative\_pos is the vector from the point to the camera in worldspace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00308}00308 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00309}00309 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_DISABLE\_TEX2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00310}00310 \textcolor{comment}{//        This disables all processing of texture 2 in the shader in case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00311}00311 \textcolor{comment}{//        you don't use it. Eventually this could be replaced with a mode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00312}00312 \textcolor{comment}{//        that omits the unused data entirely.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00313}00313 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00314}00314 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_TEX1\_EDGE\_CLAMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00315}00315 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_TEX2\_EDGE\_CLAMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00316}00316 \textcolor{comment}{//        If you want to edge clamp the textures, instead of letting them wrap,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00317}00317 \textcolor{comment}{//        set this flag. By default stb\_voxel\_render relies on texture wrapping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00318}00318 \textcolor{comment}{//        to simplify texture coordinate generation. This flag forces it to do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00319}00319 \textcolor{comment}{//        it correctly, although there can still be minor artifacts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00320}00320 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00321}00321 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_ROTATION\_IN\_LIGHTING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00322}00322 \textcolor{comment}{//        Changes the meaning of the 'lighting' mesher input variable to also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00323}00323 \textcolor{comment}{//        store the rotation; see later discussion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00324}00324 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00325}00325 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_VHEIGHT\_IN\_LIGHTING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00326}00326 \textcolor{comment}{//        Changes the meaning of the 'lighting' mesher input variable to also}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00330}00330 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_PREMULTIPLIED\_ALPHA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00331}00331 \textcolor{comment}{//        Adjusts the shader calculations on the assumption that tex1.rgba,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00332}00332 \textcolor{comment}{//        tex2.rgba, and color.rgba all use premultiplied values, and that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00333}00333 \textcolor{comment}{//        the output of the fragment shader should be premultiplied.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00334}00334 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00335}00335 \textcolor{comment}{//    STBVOX\_CONFIG\_UNPREMULTIPLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00336}00336 \textcolor{comment}{//        Only meaningful if STBVOX\_CONFIG\_PREMULTIPLIED\_ALPHA is defined.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00337}00337 \textcolor{comment}{//        Changes the behavior described above so that the inputs are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00338}00338 \textcolor{comment}{//        still premultiplied alpha, but the output of the fragment}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00339}00339 \textcolor{comment}{//        shader is not premultiplied alpha. This is needed when allowing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00340}00340 \textcolor{comment}{//        non-\/unit alpha values but not doing alpha-\/blending (for example}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00341}00341 \textcolor{comment}{//        when alpha testing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00342}00342 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00343}00343 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00345}00345 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00346}00346 \textcolor{comment}{// MESHING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00347}00347 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00348}00348 \textcolor{comment}{// A mesh represents a (typically) small chunk of a larger world.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00349}00349 \textcolor{comment}{// Meshes encode coordinates using small integers, so those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00350}00350 \textcolor{comment}{// coordinates must be relative to some base location.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00351}00351 \textcolor{comment}{// All of the coordinates in the functions below use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00352}00352 \textcolor{comment}{// these relative coordinates unless explicitly stated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00353}00353 \textcolor{comment}{// otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00354}00354 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00355}00355 \textcolor{comment}{// Input to the meshing step is documented further down}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00362}00362 STBVXDEC \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbvox\_set\_buffer(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbvox__mesh__maker}{stbvox\_mesh\_maker}} *mm, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mesh, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} slot, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *\mbox{\hyperlink{classbuffer}{buffer}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} len);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00363}00363 \textcolor{comment}{// Call this to set the buffer into which stbvox will write the mesh}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00364}00364 \textcolor{comment}{// it creates. It can build more than one mesh in parallel (distinguished}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00365}00365 \textcolor{comment}{// by the 'mesh' parameter), and each mesh can be made up of more than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00366}00366 \textcolor{comment}{// one buffer (distinguished by the 'slot' parameter).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00367}00367 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00368}00368 \textcolor{comment}{// Multiple meshes are under your control; use the 'selector' input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00369}00369 \textcolor{comment}{// variable to choose which mesh each voxel's vertices are written to.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00370}00370 \textcolor{comment}{// For example, you can use this to generate separate meshes for opaque}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00371}00371 \textcolor{comment}{// and transparent data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00372}00372 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00373}00373 \textcolor{comment}{// You can query the number of slots by calling stbvox\_get\_buffer\_count}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00374}00374 \textcolor{comment}{// described below. The meaning of the buffer for each slot depends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00375}00375 \textcolor{comment}{// on STBVOX\_CONFIG\_MODE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00376}00376 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00377}00377 \textcolor{comment}{//   In mode 0 \& mode 20, there is only one slot. The mesh data for that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00378}00378 \textcolor{comment}{//   slot is two interleaved vertex attributes: attr\_vertex, a single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00379}00379 \textcolor{comment}{//   32-\/bit uint, and attr\_face, a single 32-\/bit uint.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00380}00380 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00381}00381 \textcolor{comment}{//   In mode 1 \& mode 21, there are two slots. The first buffer should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00382}00382 \textcolor{comment}{//   be four times as large as the second buffer. The first buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00383}00383 \textcolor{comment}{//   contains a single vertex attribute: 'attr\_vertex', a single 32-\/bit uint.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00384}00384 \textcolor{comment}{//   The second buffer contains texture buffer data (an array of 32-\/bit uints)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00385}00385 \textcolor{comment}{//   that will be accessed through the sampler identified by STBVOX\_UNIFORM\_face\_data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00386}00386 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00409}00409 STBVXDEC \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbvox\_set\_input\_stride(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbvox__mesh__maker}{stbvox\_mesh\_maker}} *mm, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x\_stride\_in\_elements, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y\_stride\_in\_elements);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00410}00410 \textcolor{comment}{// This sets the stride between successive elements of the 3D arrays}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00411}00411 \textcolor{comment}{// in the stbvox\_input\_description. Z values are always stored consecutively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00412}00412 \textcolor{comment}{// (The preferred coordinate system for stbvox is X right, Y forwards, Z up.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00413}00413 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00414}00414 STBVXDEC \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbvox\_set\_input\_range(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbvox__mesh__maker}{stbvox\_mesh\_maker}} *mm, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} z0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x1, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y1, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} z1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00415}00415 \textcolor{comment}{// This sets the range of values in the 3D array for the voxels that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00416}00416 \textcolor{comment}{// the mesh generator will convert. The lower values are inclusive,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00417}00417 \textcolor{comment}{// the higher values are exclusive, so (0,0,0) to (16,16,16) generates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00418}00418 \textcolor{comment}{// mesh data associated with voxels up to (15,15,15) but no higher.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00419}00419 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00420}00420 \textcolor{comment}{// The mesh generate generates faces at the boundary between open space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00421}00421 \textcolor{comment}{// and solid space but associates them with the solid space, so if (15,0,0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00422}00422 \textcolor{comment}{// is open and (16,0,0) is solid, then the mesh will contain the boundary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00423}00423 \textcolor{comment}{// between them if x0 <= 16 and x1 > 16.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00424}00424 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00425}00425 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that the mesh generator will access array elements 1 beyond the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00426}00426 \textcolor{comment}{// limits set in these parameters. For example, if you set the limits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00427}00427 \textcolor{comment}{// to be (0,0,0) and (16,16,16), then the generator will access all of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00428}00428 \textcolor{comment}{// the voxels between (-\/1,-\/1,-\/1) and (16,16,16), including (16,16,16).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00429}00429 \textcolor{comment}{// You may have to do pointer arithmetic to make it work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00430}00430 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00431}00431 \textcolor{comment}{// For example, caveview processes mesh chunks that are 32x32x16, but it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00432}00432 \textcolor{comment}{// does this using input buffers that are 34x34x18.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00433}00433 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00434}00434 \textcolor{comment}{// The lower limits are x0 >= 0, y0 >= 0, and z0 >= 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00435}00435 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00436}00436 \textcolor{comment}{// The upper limits are mode dependent, but all the current methods are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00437}00437 \textcolor{comment}{// limited to x1 < 127, y1 < 127, z1 < 255. Note that these are not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00438}00438 \textcolor{comment}{// powers of two; if you want to use power-\/of-\/two chunks (to make}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00439}00439 \textcolor{comment}{// it efficient to decide which chunk a coordinate falls in), you're}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00440}00440 \textcolor{comment}{// limited to at most x1=64, y1=64, z1=128. For classic Minecraft-\/style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00441}00441 \textcolor{comment}{// worlds with limited vertical extent, I recommend using a single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00442}00442 \textcolor{comment}{// chunk for the entire height, which limits the height to 255 blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00443}00443 \textcolor{comment}{// (one less than Minecraft), and only chunk the map in X \& Y.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00444}00444 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00445}00445 STBVXDEC \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbvox\_make\_mesh(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbvox__mesh__maker}{stbvox\_mesh\_maker}} *mm);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00446}00446 \textcolor{comment}{// Call this function to create mesh data for the currently configured}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00447}00447 \textcolor{comment}{// set of input data. This appends to the currently configured mesh output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00448}00448 \textcolor{comment}{// buffer. Returns 1 on success. If there is not enough room in the buffer,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00449}00449 \textcolor{comment}{// it outputs as much as it can, and returns 0; you need to switch output}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00450}00450 \textcolor{comment}{// buffers (either by calling stbvox\_set\_buffer to set new buffers, or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00451}00451 \textcolor{comment}{// by copying the data out and calling stbvox\_reset\_buffers), and then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00452}00452 \textcolor{comment}{// call this function again without changing any of the input parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00453}00453 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00454}00454 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that this function appends; you can call it multiple times to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00455}00455 \textcolor{comment}{// build a single mesh. For example, caveview uses chunks that are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00456}00456 \textcolor{comment}{// 32x32x255, but builds the mesh for it by processing 32x32x16 at atime}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00457}00457 \textcolor{comment}{// (this is faster as it is reuses the same 34x34x18 input buffers rather}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00458}00458 \textcolor{comment}{// than needing 34x34x257 input buffers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00459}00459 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00460}00460 \textcolor{comment}{// Once you're done creating a mesh into a given buffer,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00461}00461 \textcolor{comment}{// consider the following functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00462}00462 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00463}00463 STBVXDEC \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbvox\_get\_quad\_count(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbvox__mesh__maker}{stbvox\_mesh\_maker}} *mm, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} mesh);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00464}00464 \textcolor{comment}{// Returns the number of quads in the mesh currently generated by mm.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00465}00465 \textcolor{comment}{// This is the sum of all consecutive stbvox\_make\_mesh runs appending}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00466}00466 \textcolor{comment}{// to the same buffer. 'mesh' distinguishes between the multiple user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00467}00467 \textcolor{comment}{// meshes available via 'selector' or stbvox\_set\_default\_mesh.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00468}00468 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00469}00469 \textcolor{comment}{// Typically you use this function when you're done building the mesh}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00470}00470 \textcolor{comment}{// and want to record how to draw it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00471}00471 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00472}00472 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that there are no index buffers; the data stored in the buffers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00473}00473 \textcolor{comment}{// should be drawn as quads (e.g. with GL\_QUAD); if your API does not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00474}00474 \textcolor{comment}{// support quads, you can create a single index buffer large enough to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00475}00475 \textcolor{comment}{// draw your largest vertex buffer, and reuse it for every rendering.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00476}00476 \textcolor{comment}{// (Note that if you use 32-\/bit indices, you'll use 24 bytes of bandwidth}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00477}00477 \textcolor{comment}{// per quad, more than the 20 bytes for the vertex/face mesh data.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00478}00478 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00497}00497 \textcolor{comment}{// translation for texture coordinate generation that avoids}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00499}00499 \textcolor{comment}{// global translation to the vertex, than multiply by modelview,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00500}00500 \textcolor{comment}{// but this means if camera location and vertex are far from the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00501}00501 \textcolor{comment}{// origin, we lose precision. Need to make a special modelview with}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00545}00545 \textcolor{comment}{//    x: scale factor to apply to texture \#1. must be a power of two. 1.0 means 'face-\/sized'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00546}00546 \textcolor{comment}{//    y: scale factor to apply to texture \#2. must be a power of two. 1.0 means 'face-\/sized'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00547}00547 \textcolor{comment}{//    z: blend mode indexed by texture \#2. 0.0 is alpha compositing; 1.0 is multiplication.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00548}00548 \textcolor{comment}{//    w: unused currently. @TODO use to support texture animation?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00549}00549 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00550}00550 \textcolor{comment}{//    Texscale is indexed by the bottom 6 or 7 bits of the texture id; thus for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00551}00551 \textcolor{comment}{//    example the texture at index 0 in the array and the texture in index 128 of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00552}00552 \textcolor{comment}{//    the array must be scaled the same. This means that if you only have 64 or 128}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00610}00610 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} setup\_uniforms(GLuint shader, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} camera\_pos[4], GLuint tex1, GLuint tex2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00611}00611 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00612}00612    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00614}00614    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i=0; i < STBVOX\_UNIFORM\_count; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00615}00615       \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbvox__uniform__info}{stbvox\_uniform\_info}} sui;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00616}00616       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (stbvox\_get\_uniform\_info(\&sui, i)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00617}00617          GLint loc = glGetUniformLocation(shader, sui.name);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00618}00618          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (loc != -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00619}00619             \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (i) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00621}00621                   glUniform4fv(loc, sui.array\_length, camera\_pos);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00622}00622                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00623}00623 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00624}00624                \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} STBVOX\_UNIFORM\_tex\_array: \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00626}00626                   glUniform1iv(loc, 2, tex\_unit);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00627}00627 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00628}00628                   glActiveTexture(GL\_TEXTURE0 + tex\_unit[0]); glBindTexture(GL\_TEXTURE\_2D\_ARRAY, tex1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00730}00730    \textcolor{comment}{// center, and the vertex light is gathered from those adjacent block}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00950}00950    \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *texlerp\_simple;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00951}00951    \textcolor{comment}{// Indexed by 3D coordinates, this is the smallest texlerp encoding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00952}00952    \textcolor{comment}{// that can do useful work. It consits of three values: baselerp,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00953}00953    \textcolor{comment}{// vertlerp, and face\_vertlerp. Baselerp defines the value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00954}00954    \textcolor{comment}{// to use on all of the faces but one, from the STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_BASE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00955}00955    \textcolor{comment}{// values. face\_vertlerp is one of the 6 face values (or STBVOX\_FACE\_NONE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00956}00956    \textcolor{comment}{// which specifies the face should use the vertlerp values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00957}00957    \textcolor{comment}{// Vertlerp defines a lerp value at every vertex of the mesh.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00958}00958    \textcolor{comment}{// Thus, one face can have per-\/vertex texlerp values, and those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00959}00959    \textcolor{comment}{// values are encoded in the space so that they will be shared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00960}00960    \textcolor{comment}{// by adjacent faces that also use vertlerp, allowing continuity}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00961}00961    \textcolor{comment}{// (this is used for the "{}texture crossfade"{} bit of the release video).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00962}00962    \textcolor{comment}{// Encode with STBVOX\_MAKE\_TEXLERP\_SIMPLE(baselerp, vertlerp, face\_vertlerp)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00963}00963 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00964}00964    \textcolor{comment}{// The following texlerp encodings are experimental and maybe not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00965}00965    \textcolor{comment}{// that useful.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00966}00966 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00967}00967    \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *texlerp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00968}00968    \textcolor{comment}{// Indexed by 3D coordinates, this defines four values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00969}00969    \textcolor{comment}{//   vertlerp is a lerp value at every vertex of the mesh (using STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_BASE values).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00970}00970    \textcolor{comment}{//   ud is the value to use on up and down faces, from STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_FACE values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00971}00971    \textcolor{comment}{//   ew is the value to use on east and west faces, from STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_FACE values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00972}00972    \textcolor{comment}{//   ns is the value to use on north and south faces, from STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_FACE values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00973}00973    \textcolor{comment}{// If any of ud, ew, or ns is STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_FACE\_use\_vert, then the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00974}00974    \textcolor{comment}{// vertlerp values for the vertices are gathered and used for those faces.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00975}00975    \textcolor{comment}{// Encode with STBVOX\_MAKE\_TEXLERP(vertlerp,ud,ew,sw)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00976}00976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00977}00977    \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} *texlerp\_vert3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00978}00978    \textcolor{comment}{// Indexed by 3D coordinates, this works with texlerp and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00979}00979    \textcolor{comment}{// provides a unique texlerp value for every direction at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00980}00980    \textcolor{comment}{// every vertex. The same rules of whether faces share values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00981}00981    \textcolor{comment}{// applies. The STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_FACE vertlerp value defined in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00982}00982    \textcolor{comment}{// texlerp is only used for the down direction. The values at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00983}00983    \textcolor{comment}{// each vertex in other directions are defined in this array,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00984}00984    \textcolor{comment}{// and each uses the STBVOX\_TEXLERP3 values (i.e. full precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00985}00985    \textcolor{comment}{// 3-\/bit texlerp values).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00986}00986    \textcolor{comment}{// Encode with STBVOX\_MAKE\_VERT3(vertlerp\_e,vertlerp\_n,vertlerp\_w,vertlerp\_s,vertlerp\_u)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00987}00987 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00988}00988    \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} *texlerp\_face3;          \textcolor{comment}{// e:3,n:3,w:3,s:3,u:2,d:2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00989}00989    \textcolor{comment}{// Indexed by 3D coordinates, this provides a compact way to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00990}00990    \textcolor{comment}{// fully specify the texlerp value indepenendly for every face,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00991}00991    \textcolor{comment}{// but doesn't allow per-\/vertex variation. E/N/W/S values are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00992}00992    \textcolor{comment}{// encoded using STBVOX\_TEXLERP3 values, whereas up and down}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00993}00993    \textcolor{comment}{// use STBVOX\_TEXLERP\_SIMPLE values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00994}00994    \textcolor{comment}{// Encode with STBVOX\_MAKE\_FACE3(face\_e,face\_n,face\_w,face\_s,face\_u,face\_d)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00995}00995 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00996}00996    \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *vheight;                 \textcolor{comment}{// STBVOX\_MAKE\_VHEIGHT   -\/-\/ sw:2, se:2, nw:2, ne:2, doesn't rotate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00997}00997    \textcolor{comment}{// Indexed by 3D coordinates, this defines the four}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00998}00998    \textcolor{comment}{// vheight values to use if the geometry is STBVOX\_GEOM\_vheight*.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l00999}00999    \textcolor{comment}{// See the vheight discussion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01000}01000 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01001}01001    \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *packed\_compact;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01002}01002    \textcolor{comment}{// Stores block rotation, vheight, and texlerp values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01003}01003    \textcolor{comment}{//    block rotation: 2 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01004}01004    \textcolor{comment}{//    vertex vheight: 2 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01005}01005    \textcolor{comment}{//    use\_texlerp   : 1 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01006}01006    \textcolor{comment}{//    vertex texlerp: 3 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01007}01007    \textcolor{comment}{// If STBVOX\_CONFIG\_UP\_TEXLERP\_PACKED is defined, then 'vertex texlerp' is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01008}01008    \textcolor{comment}{// used for up faces if use\_texlerp is 1. If STBVOX\_CONFIG\_DOWN\_TEXLERP\_PACKED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01009}01009    \textcolor{comment}{// is defined, then 'vertex texlerp' is used for down faces if use\_texlerp is 1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01010}01010    \textcolor{comment}{// Note if those symbols are defined but packed\_compact is NULL, the normal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01011}01011    \textcolor{comment}{// texlerp default will be used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01012}01012    \textcolor{comment}{// Encode with STBVOX\_MAKE\_PACKED\_COMPACT(rot, vheight, texlerp, use\_texlerp)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01013}01013 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01014}01014 \textcolor{comment}{// @OPTIMIZE allow specializing; build a single struct with all of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01015}01015 \textcolor{comment}{// 3D-\/indexed arrays combined so it's AoS instead of SoA for better}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01016}01016 \textcolor{comment}{// cache efficiency}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01017}01017 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01018}01018 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01020}01020 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01021}01021 \textcolor{comment}{//  VHEIGHT DOCUMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01022}01022 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01023}01023 \textcolor{comment}{//  "{}vheight"{} is the internal name for the special block types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01024}01024 \textcolor{comment}{//  with sloped tops or bottoms. "{}vheight"{} stands for "{}vertex height"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01025}01025 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01026}01026 \textcolor{comment}{//  Note that these blocks are very flexible (there are 256 of them,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01027}01027 \textcolor{comment}{//  although at least 17 of them should never be used), but they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01028}01028 \textcolor{comment}{//  also have a disadvantage that they generate extra invisible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01029}01029 \textcolor{comment}{//  faces; the generator does not currently detect whether adjacent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01030}01030 \textcolor{comment}{//  vheight blocks hide each others sides, so those side faces are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01031}01031 \textcolor{comment}{//  always generated. For a continuous ground terrain, this means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01032}01032 \textcolor{comment}{//  that you may generate 5x as many quads as needed. See notes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01033}01033 \textcolor{comment}{//  on "{}improvements for shipping products"{} in the introduction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01034}01034 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01035}01035 \textcolor{keyword}{enum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01036}01036 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01037}01037    STBVOX\_VERTEX\_HEIGHT\_0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01038}01038    STBVOX\_VERTEX\_HEIGHT\_half,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01039}01039    STBVOX\_VERTEX\_HEIGHT\_1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01040}01040    STBVOX\_VERTEX\_HEIGHT\_one\_and\_a\_half,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01041}01041 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01042}01042 \textcolor{comment}{// These are the "{}vheight"{} values. Vheight stands for "{}vertex height"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01043}01043 \textcolor{comment}{// The idea is that for a "{}floor vheight"{} block, you take a cube and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01044}01044 \textcolor{comment}{// reposition the top-\/most vertices at various heights as specified by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01045}01045 \textcolor{comment}{// the vheight values. Similarly, a "{}ceiling vheight"{} block takes a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01046}01046 \textcolor{comment}{// cube and repositions the bottom-\/most vertices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01047}01047 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01048}01048 \textcolor{comment}{// A floor block only adjusts the top four vertices; the bottom four vertices}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01049}01049 \textcolor{comment}{// remain at the bottom of the block. The height values are 2 bits,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01050}01050 \textcolor{comment}{// measured in halves of a block; so you can specify heights of 0/2,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01051}01051 \textcolor{comment}{// 1/2, 2/2, or 3/2. 0 is the bottom of the block, 1 is halfway}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01052}01052 \textcolor{comment}{// up the block, 2 is the top of the block, and 3 is halfway up the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01053}01053 \textcolor{comment}{// next block (and actually outside of the block). The value 3 is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01054}01054 \textcolor{comment}{// actually legal for floor vheight (but not ceiling), and allows you to:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01055}01055 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01056}01056 \textcolor{comment}{//     (A) have smoother terrain by having slopes that cross blocks,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01057}01057 \textcolor{comment}{//         e.g. (1,1,3,3) is a regular-\/seeming slope halfway between blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01058}01058 \textcolor{comment}{//     (B) make slopes steeper than 45-\/degrees, e.g. (0,0,3,3)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01059}01059 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01060}01060 \textcolor{comment}{// (Because only z coordinates have half-\/block precision, and x\&y are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01061}01061 \textcolor{comment}{// limited to block corner precision, it's not possible to make these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01062}01062 \textcolor{comment}{// things "{}properly"{} out of blocks, e.g. a half-\/slope block on its side}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01063}01063 \textcolor{comment}{// or a sloped block halfway between blocks that's made out of two blocks.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01064}01064 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01065}01065 \textcolor{comment}{// If you define STBVOX\_CONFIG\_OPTIMIZED\_VHEIGHT, then the top face}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01066}01066 \textcolor{comment}{// (or bottom face for a ceiling vheight block) will be drawn as a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01067}01067 \textcolor{comment}{// single quad even if the four vertex heights aren't planar, and a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01068}01068 \textcolor{comment}{// single normal will be used over the entire quad. If you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01069}01069 \textcolor{comment}{// don't define it, then if the top face is non-\/planar, it will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01070}01070 \textcolor{comment}{// split into two triangles, each with their own normal/lighting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01071}01071 \textcolor{comment}{// (Note that since all output from stb\_voxel\_render is quad meshes,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01072}01072 \textcolor{comment}{// triangles are actually rendered as degenerate quads.) In this case,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01073}01073 \textcolor{comment}{// the distinction between STBVOX\_GEOM\_floor\_vheight\_03 and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01074}01074 \textcolor{comment}{// STBVOX\_GEOM\_floor\_vheight\_12 comes into play; the former introduces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01075}01075 \textcolor{comment}{// an edge from the SW to NE corner (i.e. from <0,0,?> to <1,1,?>),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01076}01076 \textcolor{comment}{// while the latter introduces an edge from the NW to SE corner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01077}01077 \textcolor{comment}{// (i.e. from <0,1,?> to <1,0,?>.) For a "{}lazy mesh"{} look, use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01078}01078 \textcolor{comment}{// exclusively \_03 or \_12. For a "{}classic mesh"{} look, alternate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01079}01079 \textcolor{comment}{// \_03 and \_12 in a checkerboard pattern. For a "{}smoothest surface"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01080}01080 \textcolor{comment}{// look, choose the edge based on actual vertex heights.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01081}01081 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01082}01082 \textcolor{comment}{// The four vertex heights can come from several places. The simplest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01083}01083 \textcolor{comment}{// encoding is to just use the 'vheight' parameter which stores four}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01084}01084 \textcolor{comment}{// explicit vertex heights for every block. This allows total independence,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01085}01085 \textcolor{comment}{// but at the cost of the largest memory usage, 1 byte per 3D block.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01086}01086 \textcolor{comment}{// Encode this with STBVOX\_MAKE\_VHEIGHT(vh\_sw, vh\_se, vh\_nw, vh\_ne).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01087}01087 \textcolor{comment}{// These coordinates are absolute, not affected by block rotations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01088}01088 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01089}01089 \textcolor{comment}{// An alternative if you just want to encode some very specific block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01090}01090 \textcolor{comment}{// types, not all the possibilities-\/-\/say you just want half-\/height slopes,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01091}01091 \textcolor{comment}{// so you want (0,0,1,1) and (1,1,2,2)-\/-\/then you can use block\_vheight}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01092}01092 \textcolor{comment}{// to specify them. The geometry rotation will cause block\_vheight values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01093}01093 \textcolor{comment}{// to be rotated (because it's as if you're just defining a type of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01094}01094 \textcolor{comment}{// block). This value is also encoded with STBVOX\_MAKE\_VHEIGHT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01095}01095 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01096}01096 \textcolor{comment}{// If you want to save memory and you're creating a "{}continuous ground"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01097}01097 \textcolor{comment}{// sort of effect, you can make each vertex of the lattice share the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01098}01098 \textcolor{comment}{// vheight value; that is, two adjacent blocks that share a vertex will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01099}01099 \textcolor{comment}{// always get the same vheight value for that vertex. Then you need to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01100}01100 \textcolor{comment}{// store two bits of vheight for every block, which you do by storing it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01101}01101 \textcolor{comment}{// as part another data structure. Store the south-\/west vertex's vheight}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01102}01102 \textcolor{comment}{// with the block. You can either use the "{}geometry"{} mesh variable (it's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01103}01103 \textcolor{comment}{// a parameter to STBVOX\_MAKE\_GEOMETRY) or you can store it in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01104}01104 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}lighting"{} mesh variable if you defined STBVOX\_CONFIG\_VHEIGHT\_IN\_LIGHTING,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01105}01105 \textcolor{comment}{// using STBVOX\_MAKE\_LIGHTING\_EXT(lighting,vheight).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01106}01106 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01107}01107 \textcolor{comment}{// Note that if you start with a 2D height map and generate vheight data from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01108}01108 \textcolor{comment}{// it, you don't necessarily store only one value per (x,y) coordinate,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01109}01109 \textcolor{comment}{// as the same value may need to be set up at multiple z heights. For}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01110}01110 \textcolor{comment}{// example, if height(8,8) = 13.5, then you want the block at (8,8,13)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01111}01111 \textcolor{comment}{// to store STBVOX\_VERTEX\_HEIGHT\_half, and this will be used by blocks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01112}01112 \textcolor{comment}{// at (7,7,13), (8,7,13), (7,8,13), and (8,8,13). However, if you're}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01113}01113 \textcolor{comment}{// allowing steep slopes, it might be the case that you have a block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01114}01114 \textcolor{comment}{// at (7,7,12) which is supposed to stick up to 13.5; that means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__voxel__render_8h_source_l01115}01115 \textcolor{comment}{// you also need to store STBVOX\_VERTEX\_HEIGHT\_one\_and\_a\_half at (8,8,12).}}
